    WHERE [d].[DriverType] = N'Auto'
) AS [t1] ON [t].[Id] = [t1].[QuoteId]

    SELECT TOP(1) [q].[Id], [q].[AdditionalComments], [q].[Address], [q].[City], [q].[ClaimsIn3Years], [q].[ContinuousCoverage], [q].[Country], [q].[CoverageDesired], [q].[CreatedDate], [q].[CurrentInsuranceCompany], [q].[Email], [q].[FirstName], [q].[InformationSecure], [q].[LastName], [q].[PhoneNumber], [q].[PolicyExpiresIn], [q].[QuoteNumber], [q].[QuoteType], [q].[State], [q].[Status], [q].[TicketsIn3Years], [q].[UpdatedDate], [q].[WhenToStart], [q].[ZipCode], [m].[QuoteId]

    LEFT JOIN [MotorcycleQuotes] AS [m] ON [q].[Id] = [m].[QuoteId]

) AS [t]

ORDER BY [t].[Id], [t].[QuoteId], [v].[Id]
